Saṃyutta Nikāya
4. Saḷāyatana Vagga
40. Moggallāna Saṃyutta

Sutta 11

Candano, Suyāma, Santusita, Sunimmita, Vasavatti

Adapted from the 1995 edition of the digital version of the Sri Lanka Buddha Jayanti Tripitaka Series.

 

I

Candano

 

[1][pts] Evaṃ me sutaṃ:|| ||

Ekaṃ samayaṃ āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno Sāvatthiyaṃ viharati Jetavane Anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme.|| ||

Atha kho āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno seyyathā pi nāma balavā puriso sammiñjitaṃ vā bāhaṃ pasāreyya pasāritaṃ vā bāhaṃ sammiñjeyya,||
evam eva Jetavane antara-hito devesu Tāvatiṃsesu pātur ahosi.|| ||

Atha kho Candano devputto pañcahi devatāsatehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami,||
upasaṇkamitvā āyasmantaṃ Mahā Moggallānaṃ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaṃ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaṃ ṭhitaṃ kho Candano devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Buddha saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

■

"Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanahete kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

 

§

 

Atha kho Candano devputto chahi devatāsatehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami,||
upasaṇkamitvā āyasmantaṃ Mahā Moggallānaṃ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaṃ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaṃ ṭhitaṃ kho Candano devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Buddha saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

■

"Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanahete kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

 

§

 

Atha kho Candano devputto sattahi devatāsatehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami,||
upasaṇkamitvā āyasmantaṃ Mahā Moggallānaṃ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaṃ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaṃ ṭhitaṃ kho Candano devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Buddha saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

■

"Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanahete kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

 

§

 

Atha kho Candano devputto aṭṭhahi devatāsatehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami,||
upasaṇkamitvā āyasmantaṃ Mahā Moggallānaṃ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaṃ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaṃ ṭhitaṃ kho Candano devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Buddha saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

■

"Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanahete kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

 

§

 

Atha kho Candano devputto asītiyā devatāsahassehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami,||
upasaṇkamitvā āyasmantaṃ Mahā Moggallānaṃ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaṃ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaṃ ṭhitaṃ kho Candano devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Buddha saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

■

"Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanahete kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

 

2.

 

Atha kho Candano devputto pañcahi devatāsatehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami.|| ||

Upasaṇkamitvā āyasmantaṃ Mahā Moggallānaṃ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaṃ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaṃ ṭhitaṃ kho Candano devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Iti pi so Bhagavā||
Arahaṃ||
Sammā Sambuddho||
vijjā-caraṇa-sampanno||
Sugato||
loka-vidū||
anuttaro purisa-damma-sārathī||
sattā deva-manussānaṃ||
Buddho||
Bhagavā' ti.|| ||

Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Svākhyāto Bhagavatā Dhammo sandiṭṭhiko||
akāliko||
ehi passiko||
opanayiko||
paccattaṃ||
veditabbo viññūhī' ti|| ||

Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Su-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
uju-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
ñāya-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
sāmīci-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho,||
yad idaṃ cattāri purisa-yugāni||
aṭṭhapurisa-puggalā.|| ||

Esa Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho.|| ||

Āhuneyo||
pāhuneyyo||
dakkhiṇeyyo||
añjali-karaṇīyo||
anuttaraṃ puñña-k-khettaṃ lokassā' ti.|| ||

Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Akhaṇḍehi||
acchiddehi||
asabalehi||
akammāsehi||
bhujissehi||
viññūppasatthehi;||
aparām-aṭṭhehi samādhi-saṃvaṭṭanikehi' ti.|| ||

Ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

■

"Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Iti pi so Bhagavā||
Arahaṃ||
Sammā Sambuddho||
vijjā-caraṇa-sampanno||
Sugato||
loka-vidū||
anuttaro purisa-damma-sārathī||
sattā deva-manussānaṃ||
Buddho||
Bhagavā' ti.|| ||

Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti,|| ||

'Svākhyāto Bhagavatā Dhammo sandiṭṭhiko||
akāliko||
ehi passiko||
opanayiko||
paccattaṃ||
veditabbo viññūhī' ti|| ||

Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Su-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
uju-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
ñāya-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
sāmīci-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho,||
yad idaṃ cattāri purisa-yugāni||
aṭṭhapurisa-puggalā.|| ||

Esa Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho.|| ||

Āhuneyo||
pāhuneyyo||
dakkhiṇeyyo||
añjali-karaṇīyo||
anuttaraṃ puñña-k-khettaṃ lokassā' ti.|| ||

Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Akhaṇḍehi||
acchiddehi||
asabalehi||
akammāsehi||
bhujissehi||
viññūppasatthehi;||
aparām-aṭṭhehi samādhi-saṃvaṭṭanikehi' ti.|| ||

Ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

 

§

 

Atha kho Candano devputto chahi devatāsatehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami.|| ||

sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho devputto Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

aṭṭhapurisa-puggalā.|| ||

Esa Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho.|| ||

Āhuneyo||
pāhuneyyo||
dakkhiṇeyyo||
añjali-karaṇīyo||
anuttaraṃ puñña-k-khettaṃ lokassā' ti.|| ||

Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Akhaṇḍehi||
acchiddehi||
asabalehi||
akammāsehi||
bhujissehi||
viññūppasatthehi;||
aparām-aṭṭhehi samādhi-saṃvaṭṭanikehi' ti.|| ||

Ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

■

"Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Iti pi so Bhagavā||
Arahaṃ||
Sammā Sambuddho||
vijjā-caraṇa-sampanno||
Sugato||
loka-vidū||
anuttaro purisa-damma-sārathī||
sattā deva-manussānaṃ||
Buddho||
Bhagavā' ti.|| ||

Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti,|| ||

'Svākhyāto Bhagavatā Dhammo sandiṭṭhiko||
akāliko||
ehi passiko||
opanayiko||
paccattaṃ||
veditabbo viññūhī' ti|| ||

Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Su-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
uju-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
ñāya-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
sāmīci-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho,||
yad idaṃ cattāri purisa-yugāni||
aṭṭhapurisa-puggalā.|| ||

Esa Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho.|| ||

Āhuneyo||
pāhuneyyo||
dakkhiṇeyyo||
añjali-karaṇīyo||
anuttaraṃ puñña-k-khettaṃ lokassā' ti.|| ||

Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Akhaṇḍehi||
acchiddehi||
asabalehi||
akammāsehi||
bhujissehi||
viññūppasatthehi;||
aparām-aṭṭhehi samādhi-saṃvaṭṭanikehi' ti.|| ||

Ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

3.

 

Atha kho āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno seyyathā pi nāma balavā puriso sammiñjitaṃ vā bāhaṃ pasāreyya pasāritaṃ vā bāhaṃ sammiñjeyya,||
evam eva Jetavane antara-hito devesu Tāvatiṃsesu pātur ahosi.|| ||

Atha kho Candano devputto pañcahi devatāsatehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami,||
upasaṇkamitvā āyasmantaṃ Mahā Moggallānaṃ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaṃ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaṃ ṭhitaṃ kho Candano devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti.|| ||

Buddha saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti.

Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti.|| ||

Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi" ti.|| ||

 

4.

 

Atha kho Candano devputto pañcahi devatāsatehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami.|| ||

Upasaṇkamitvā āyasmantaṃ Mahā Moggallānaṃ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaṃ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaṃ ṭhitaṃ kho Candano devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Iti pi so Bhagavā||
arahaṃ||
Arahaṃ||
Sammā Sambuddho||
vijjā-caraṇa-sampanno||
Sugato||
loka-vidū||
anuttaro purisa-damma-sārathī||
sattā deva-manussānaṃ||
Buddho||
Bhagavā' ti.|| ||

Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantti|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Svākhyāto Bhagavatā Dhammo||
sandiṭṭhiko||
akāliko||
ehi passiko||
opanayiko||
paccattaṃ||
veditabbo viññūhī' ti|| ||

Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||

dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

'Su-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
uju-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
ñāya-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
sāmīci-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho,||
yad idaṃ cattāri purisa-yugāni||
aṭṭhapurisa-puggalā.|| ||

Esa Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho.|| ||

Āhuneyo||
pāhuneyyo||
dakkhiṇeyyo||
añjali-karaṇīyo||
anuttaraṃ puñña-k-khettaṃ lokassā' ti.|| ||

Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Akhaṇḍehi||
acchiddehi||
asabalehi||
akammāsehi||
bhujissehi||
viññūppasatthehi;||
aparām-aṭṭhehi samādhi-saṃvaṭṭanikehi' ti.|| ||

Ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi" ti.|| ||

 

II

Suyāma

 

Atha kho Suyāma devputto pañcahi devatāsatehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami,||
upasaṇkamitvā āyasmantaṃ Mahā Moggallānaṃ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaṃ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaṃ ṭhitaṃ kho Suyāma devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Buddha saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

■

"Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanahete kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

 

§

 

Atha kho Suyāma devputto chahi devatāsatehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami,||
upasaṇkamitvā āyasmantaṃ Mahā Moggallānaṃ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaṃ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

evam idh'ekacce sattā||

sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||

evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||

evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

2.

 

Atha kho Suyāma devputto pañcahi devatāsatehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami.|| ||

Upasaṇkamitvā āyasmantaṃ Mahā Moggallānaṃ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaṃ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaṃ ṭhitaṃ kho Suyāma devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Iti pi so Bhagavā||
Arahaṃ||
Sammā Sambuddho||
vijjā-caraṇa-sampanno||
Sugato||
loka-vidū||
anuttaro purisa-damma-sārathī||
sattā deva-manussānaṃ||
Buddho||
Bhagavā' ti.|| ||

Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Svākhyāto Bhagavatā Dhammo sandiṭṭhiko||
akāliko||
ehi passiko||
opanayiko||
paccattaṃ||
veditabbo viññūhī' ti|| ||

Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

aṭṭhapurisa-puggalā.|| ||

pāhuneyyo||
dakkhiṇeyyo||
añjali-karaṇīyo||
anuttaraṃ puñña-k-khettaṃ lokassā' ti.|| ||

Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

3.

 

Atha kho āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno seyyathā pi nāma balavā puriso sammiñjitaṃ vā bāhaṃ pasāreyya pasāritaṃ vā bāhaṃ sammiñjeyya,||
evam eva Jetavane antara-hito devesu Tāvatiṃsesu pātur ahosi.|| ||

Atha kho Suyāma devputto pañcahi devatāsatehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami,||
upasaṇkamitvā āyasmantaṃ Mahā Moggallānaṃ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaṃ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaṃ ṭhitaṃ kho Suyāma devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti.|| ||

Buddha saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti.|| ||

Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanahete kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti.|| ||

Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjant.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi" ti.|| ||

 

4.

 

Atha kho Suyāma devputto pañcahi devatāsatehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami.|| ||

Upasaṇkamitvā āyasmantaṃ Mahā Moggallānaṃ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaṃ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaṃ ṭhitaṃ kho Suyāma devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Iti pi so Bhagavā||
arahaṃ||
Arahaṃ||
Sammā Sambuddho||
vijjā-caraṇa-sampanno||
Sugato||
loka-vidū||
anuttaro purisa-damma-sārathī||
sattā deva-manussānaṃ||
Buddho||
Bhagavā' ti.|| ||

Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantti|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Svākhyāto Bhagavatā Dhammo||
sandiṭṭhiko||
akāliko||
ehi passiko||
opanayiko||
paccattaṃ||
veditabbo viññūhī' ti|| ||

Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||

sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti|| ||

acchiddehi||

Sādhu kho devputto Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Svākhyāto Bhagavatā Dhammo||
sandiṭṭhiko||
akāliko||
ehi passiko||
opanayiko||
paccattaṃ||
veditabbo viññūhī' ti|| ||

Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Su-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
uju-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
ñāya-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
sāmīci-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho,||
yad idaṃ cattāri purisa-yugāni||
aṭṭhapurisa-puggalā.|| ||

Esa Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho.|| ||

Āhuneyo||
pāhuneyyo||
dakkhiṇeyyo||
añjali-karaṇīyo||
anuttaraṃ puñña-k-khettaṃ lokassā' ti.|| ||

Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||

dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

'Akhaṇḍehi||
acchiddehi||
asabalehi||
akammāsehi||
bhujissehi||
viññūppasatthehi;||
aparām-aṭṭhehi samādhi-saṃvaṭṭanikehi' ti.|| ||

Ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||

Atha kho Suyāma devputto aṭṭhahi devatāsatehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami.|| ||

sattā deva-manussānaṃ||
Buddho||
Bhagavā' ti.|| ||

Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantti|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti,|| ||

'Svākhyāto Bhagavatā Dhammo||
sandiṭṭhiko||
akāliko||
ehi passiko||
opanayiko||
paccattaṃ||
veditabbo viññūhī' ti|| ||

Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti,|| ||

'Su-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
uju-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
ñāya-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
sāmīci-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho,||
yad idaṃ cattāri purisa-yugāni||
aṭṭhapurisa-puggalā.|| ||

Esa Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho.|| ||

Āhuneyo||
pāhuneyyo||
dakkhiṇeyyo||
añjali-karaṇīyo||
anuttaraṃ puñña-k-khettaṃ lokassā' ti.|| ||

Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Akhaṇḍehi||
acchiddehi||
asabalehi||
akammāsehi||
bhujissehi||
viññūppasatthehi;||
aparām-aṭṭhehi samādhi-saṃvaṭṭanikehi' ti.|| ||

Ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi" ti.|| ||

 

III

Santusita

 

Atha kho Santusita devputto pañcahi devatāsatehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami,||
upasaṇkamitvā āyasmantaṃ Mahā Moggallānaṃ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaṃ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaṃ ṭhitaṃ kho Santusita devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Buddha saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

■

"Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanahete kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

 

§

 

Atha kho Santusita devputto chahi devatāsatehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami,||
upasaṇkamitvā āyasmantaṃ Mahā Moggallānaṃ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaṃ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaṃ ṭhitaṃ kho Santusita devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

evam idh'ekacce sattā||

sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||

evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||

evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

Upasaṇkamitvā āyasmantaṃ Mahā Moggallānaṃ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaṃ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaṃ ṭhitaṃ kho Santusita devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Iti pi so Bhagavā||
Arahaṃ||
Sammā Sambuddho||
vijjā-caraṇa-sampanno||
Sugato||
loka-vidū||
anuttaro purisa-damma-sārathī||
sattā deva-manussānaṃ||
Buddho||
Bhagavā' ti.|| ||

Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Svākhyāto Bhagavatā Dhammo sandiṭṭhiko||
akāliko||
ehi passiko||
opanayiko||
paccattaṃ||
veditabbo viññūhī' ti|| ||

Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

'Su-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
uju-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
ñāya-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
sāmīci-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho,||
yad idaṃ cattāri purisa-yugāni||
aṭṭhapurisa-puggalā.|| ||

Esa Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho.|| ||

Āhuneyo||
pāhuneyyo||
dakkhiṇeyyo||
añjali-karaṇīyo||
anuttaraṃ puñña-k-khettaṃ lokassā' ti.|| ||

Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Akhaṇḍehi||
acchiddehi||
asabalehi||
akammāsehi||
bhujissehi||
viññūppasatthehi;||
aparām-aṭṭhehi samādhi-saṃvaṭṭanikehi' ti.|| ||

sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

Esa Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho.|| ||

Āhuneyo||
pāhuneyyo||
dakkhiṇeyyo||
añjali-karaṇīyo||
anuttaraṃ puñña-k-khettaṃ lokassā' ti.|| ||

Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Akhaṇḍehi||
acchiddehi||
asabalehi||
akammāsehi||
bhujissehi||
viññūppasatthehi;||
aparām-aṭṭhehi samādhi-saṃvaṭṭanikehi' ti.|| ||

Ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

 

3.

 

Atha kho āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno seyyathā pi nāma balavā puriso sammiñjitaṃ vā bāhaṃ pasāreyya pasāritaṃ vā bāhaṃ sammiñjeyya,||
evam eva Jetavane antara-hito devesu Tāvatiṃsesu pātur ahosi.|| ||

Atha kho Santusita devputto pañcahi devatāsatehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami,||
upasaṇkamitvā āyasmantaṃ Mahā Moggallānaṃ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaṃ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaṃ ṭhitaṃ kho Santusita devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti.|| ||

Buddha saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti.

Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti.|| ||

Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||

dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi" ti.|| ||

Atha kho Santusita devputto pañcahi devatāsatehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami.|| ||

Bhagavā' ti.|| ||

dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi" ti.|| ||

 

§

 

Atha kho Santusita devputto sattahi devatāsatehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami.|| ||

Upasaṇkamitvā āyasmantaṃ Mahā Moggallānaṃ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaṃ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaṃ ṭhitaṃ kho Santusita devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Iti pi so Bhagavā||
arahaṃ||
Arahaṃ||
Sammā Sambuddho||
vijjā-caraṇa-sampanno||

loka-vidū||

sattā deva-manussānaṃ||
Buddho||
Bhagavā' ti.|| ||

Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantti|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Akhaṇḍehi||
acchiddehi||
asabalehi||
akammāsehi||
bhujissehi||
viññūppasatthehi;||
aparām-aṭṭhehi samādhi-saṃvaṭṭanikehi' ti.|| ||

Ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi" ti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti,|| ||

'Iti pi so Bhagavā||
arahaṃ||
Arahaṃ||
Sammā Sambuddho||
vijjā-caraṇa-sampanno||
Sugato||
loka-vidū||
anuttaro purisa-damma-sārathī||
sattā deva-manussānaṃ||
Buddho||
Bhagavā' ti.|| ||

Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantti|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti,|| ||

'Svākhyāto Bhagavatā Dhammo||
sandiṭṭhiko||
akāliko||
ehi passiko||
opanayiko||
paccattaṃ||
veditabbo viññūhī' ti|| ||

Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti,|| ||

'Su-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
uju-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
ñāya-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
sāmīci-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho,||
yad idaṃ cattāri purisa-yugāni||
aṭṭhapurisa-puggalā.|| ||

Esa Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho.|| ||

Āhuneyo||
pāhuneyyo||
dakkhiṇeyyo||
añjali-karaṇīyo||
anuttaraṃ puñña-k-khettaṃ lokassā' ti.|| ||

Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||

dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Akhaṇḍehi||
acchiddehi||
asabalehi||
akammāsehi||
bhujissehi||
viññūppasatthehi;||
aparām-aṭṭhehi samādhi-saṃvaṭṭanikehi' ti.|| ||

Ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi" ti.|| ||

 

IV

Sunimmita

 

Atha kho Sunimmita devputto pañcahi devatāsatehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami,||
upasaṇkamitvā āyasmantaṃ Mahā Moggallānaṃ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaṃ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaṃ ṭhitaṃ kho Sunimmita devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Buddha saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

■

"Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanahete kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

 

§

 

Atha kho Sunimmita devputto chahi devatāsatehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami,||
upasaṇkamitvā āyasmantaṃ Mahā Moggallānaṃ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaṃ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaṃ ṭhitaṃ kho Sunimmita devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Buddha saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

■

"Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanahete kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

 

§

 

Atha kho Sunimmita devputto sattahi devatāsatehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami,||

Eka-m-antaṃ ṭhitaṃ kho Sunimmita devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

Atha kho Sunimmita devputto asītiyā devatāsahassehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami,||

sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

 

2.

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Su-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
uju-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
ñāya-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
sāmīci-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho,||
yad idaṃ cattāri purisa-yugāni||
aṭṭhapurisa-puggalā.|| ||

Esa Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho.|| ||

Āhuneyo||
pāhuneyyo||
dakkhiṇeyyo||
añjali-karaṇīyo||
anuttaraṃ puñña-k-khettaṃ lokassā' ti.|| ||

Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Akhaṇḍehi||
acchiddehi||
asabalehi||
akammāsehi||
bhujissehi||
viññūppasatthehi;||
aparām-aṭṭhehi samādhi-saṃvaṭṭanikehi' ti.|| ||

Ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

■

"Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Iti pi so Bhagavā||
Arahaṃ||
Sammā Sambuddho||
vijjā-caraṇa-sampanno||
Sugato||
loka-vidū||
anuttaro purisa-damma-sārathī||
sattā deva-manussānaṃ||
Buddho||
Bhagavā' ti.|| ||

Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti,|| ||

'Svākhyāto Bhagavatā Dhammo sandiṭṭhiko||
akāliko||
ehi passiko||
opanayiko||
paccattaṃ||
veditabbo viññūhī' ti|| ||

Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Su-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
uju-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
ñāya-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
sāmīci-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho,||
yad idaṃ cattāri purisa-yugāni||
aṭṭhapurisa-puggalā.|| ||

Esa Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho.|| ||

Āhuneyo||
pāhuneyyo||
dakkhiṇeyyo||
añjali-karaṇīyo||
anuttaraṃ puñña-k-khettaṃ lokassā' ti.|| ||

Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Akhaṇḍehi||
acchiddehi||
asabalehi||
akammāsehi||
bhujissehi||
viññūppasatthehi;||
aparām-aṭṭhehi samādhi-saṃvaṭṭanikehi' ti.|| ||

Ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

 

3.

 

Atha kho āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno seyyathā pi nāma balavā puriso sammiñjitaṃ vā bāhaṃ pasāreyya pasāritaṃ vā bāhaṃ sammiñjeyya,||
evam eva Jetavane antara-hito devesu Tāvatiṃsesu pātur ahosi.|| ||

Atha kho Sunimmita devputto pañcahi devatāsatehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami,||
upasaṇkamitvā āyasmantaṃ Mahā Moggallānaṃ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaṃ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaṃ ṭhitaṃ kho Sunimmita devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti.|| ||

Buddha saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjant.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi" ti.|| ||

 

§

 

Atha kho Sunimmita devputto asītiyā devatāsahassehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami,||
upasaṇkamitvā āyasmantaṃ Mahā Moggallānaṃ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaṃ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

4.

 

Atha kho Sunimmita devputto pañcahi devatāsatehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami.|| ||

Eka-m-antaṃ ṭhitaṃ kho Sunimmita devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Iti pi so Bhagavā||
arahaṃ||
Arahaṃ||
Sammā Sambuddho||
vijjā-caraṇa-sampanno||
Sugato||
loka-vidū||
anuttaro purisa-damma-sārathī||
sattā deva-manussānaṃ||
Buddho||
Bhagavā' ti.|| ||

Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantti|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||

dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

sandiṭṭhiko||
akāliko||
ehi passiko||
opanayiko||
paccattaṃ||
veditabbo viññūhī' ti|| ||

yad idaṃ cattāri purisa-yugāni||
aṭṭhapurisa-puggalā.|| ||

Esa Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho.|| ||

Āhuneyo||
pāhuneyyo||
dakkhiṇeyyo||
añjali-karaṇīyo||
anuttaraṃ puñña-k-khettaṃ lokassā' ti.|| ||

Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Akhaṇḍehi||
acchiddehi||
asabalehi||
akammāsehi||
bhujissehi||
viññūppasatthehi;||
aparām-aṭṭhehi samādhi-saṃvaṭṭanikehi' ti.|| ||

Ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||

dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi" ti.|| ||

dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

Sādhu kho devputto Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Svākhyāto Bhagavatā Dhammo||
sandiṭṭhiko||
akāliko||
ehi passiko||
opanayiko||
paccattaṃ||
veditabbo viññūhī' ti|| ||

Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Su-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
uju-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
ñāya-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
sāmīci-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho,||
yad idaṃ cattāri purisa-yugāni||
aṭṭhapurisa-puggalā.|| ||

Esa Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho.|| ||

Āhuneyo||
pāhuneyyo||
dakkhiṇeyyo||
añjali-karaṇīyo||
anuttaraṃ puñña-k-khettaṃ lokassā' ti.|| ||

Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Akhaṇḍehi||
acchiddehi||
asabalehi||
akammāsehi||
bhujissehi||
viññūppasatthehi;||
aparām-aṭṭhehi samādhi-saṃvaṭṭanikehi' ti.|| ||

Ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||

dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi" ti.|| ||

V

Vasavatti

 

Atha kho Vasavatti devputto pañcahi devatāsatehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami,||
upasaṇkamitvā āyasmantaṃ Mahā Moggallānaṃ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaṃ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaṃ ṭhitaṃ kho Vasavatti devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Buddha saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

■

"Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanahete kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti,||
Saṇghaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

 

§

2.

 

Atha kho Vasavatti devputto pañcahi devatāsatehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami.|| ||

Eka-m-antaṃ ṭhitaṃ kho Vasavatti devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Iti pi so Bhagavā||
Arahaṃ||
Sammā Sambuddho||
vijjā-caraṇa-sampanno||
Sugato||
loka-vidū||
anuttaro purisa-damma-sārathī||
sattā deva-manussānaṃ||
Buddho||
Bhagavā' ti.|| ||

Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Svākhyāto Bhagavatā Dhammo sandiṭṭhiko||
akāliko||
ehi passiko||
opanayiko||
paccattaṃ||
veditabbo viññūhī' ti|| ||

Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Su-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
uju-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
ñāya-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
sāmīci-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho,||
yad idaṃ cattāri purisa-yugāni||
aṭṭhapurisa-puggalā.|| ||

Esa Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho.|| ||

Āhuneyo||
pāhuneyyo||
dakkhiṇeyyo||
añjali-karaṇīyo||
anuttaraṃ puñña-k-khettaṃ lokassā' ti.|| ||

Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

paccattaṃ||
veditabbo viññūhī' ti|| ||

Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Su-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
uju-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
ñāya-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
sāmīci-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho,||
yad idaṃ cattāri purisa-yugāni||
aṭṭhapurisa-puggalā.|| ||

Esa Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho.|| ||

Āhuneyo||
pāhuneyyo||
dakkhiṇeyyo||
añjali-karaṇīyo||
anuttaraṃ puñña-k-khettaṃ lokassā' ti.|| ||

Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Akhaṇḍehi||
acchiddehi||
asabalehi||
akammāsehi||
bhujissehi||
viññūppasatthehi;||
aparām-aṭṭhehi samādhi-saṃvaṭṭanikehi' ti.|| ||

Ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

■

"Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Iti pi so Bhagavā||
Arahaṃ||
Sammā Sambuddho||
vijjā-caraṇa-sampanno||
Sugato||
loka-vidū||
anuttaro purisa-damma-sārathī||
sattā deva-manussānaṃ||
Buddho||
Bhagavā' ti.|| ||

Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti,|| ||

akāliko||
ehi passiko||
opanayiko||
paccattaṃ||
veditabbo viññūhī' ti|| ||

kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

3.

 

Atha kho āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno seyyathā pi nāma balavā puriso sammiñjitaṃ vā bāhaṃ pasāreyya pasāritaṃ vā bāhaṃ sammiñjeyya,||
evam eva Jetavane antara-hito devesu Tāvatiṃsesu pātur ahosi.|| ||

Atha kho Vasavatti devputto pañcahi devatāsatehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami,||
upasaṇkamitvā āyasmantaṃ Mahā Moggallānaṃ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaṃ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaṃ ṭhitaṃ kho Vasavatti devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti.|| ||

Buddha saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti.

Dhammaṃ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||

dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi" ti.|| ||

"Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhaṃ saraṇa-gamanaṃ hoti.|| ||

dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

opanayiko||
paccattaṃ||
veditabbo viññūhī' ti|| ||

sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti|| ||

anuttaraṃ puñña-k-khettaṃ lokassā' ti.|| ||

§

 

Atha kho Vasavatti devputto asītiyā devatāsahassehi saddhiṃ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasaṇkami.|| ||

Upasaṇkamitvā āyasmantaṃ Mahā Moggallānaṃ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaṃ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaṃ ṭhitaṃ kho Vasavatti devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Iti pi so Bhagavā||
arahaṃ||
Arahaṃ||
Sammā Sambuddho||
vijjā-caraṇa-sampanno||
Sugato||
loka-vidū||
anuttaro purisa-damma-sārathī||
sattā deva-manussānaṃ||
Buddho||
Bhagavā' ti.|| ||

Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantti|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Svākhyāto Bhagavatā Dhammo||
sandiṭṭhiko||
akāliko||
ehi passiko||
opanayiko||
paccattaṃ||
veditabbo viññūhī' ti|| ||

Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Su-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
uju-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
ñāya-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho||
sāmīci-paṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho,||
yad idaṃ cattāri purisa-yugāni||
aṭṭhapurisa-puggalā.|| ||

Esa Bhagavato sāvaka-saṇgho.|| ||

Āhuneyo||
pāhuneyyo||
dakkhiṇeyyo||
añjali-karaṇīyo||
anuttaraṃ puñña-k-khettaṃ lokassā' ti.|| ||

Saṇghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjanti.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamanaṃ hoti:|| ||

'Akhaṇḍehi||
acchiddehi||
asabalehi||
akammāsehi||
bhujissehi||
viññūppasatthehi;||
aparām-aṭṭhehi samādhi-saṃvaṭṭanikehi' ti.|| ||

Ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantī.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi" ti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaṃ hoti,|| ||

Bhagavā' ti.|| ||

sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajjantti|| ||
